Management</p><p>(BA)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="4"><p>中級會計學(一)</p><p>CM220(3)</p><p>(會計)</p><p>Intermediate Accounting(I)</p><p>(AC)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>投資學*</p><p>CM222(3)</p><p>(財金)</p><p>Investments</p><p>(FN)</p></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="2"><p>公司理財*</p><p>CM223(3)</p><p>(財金)</p><p>Corporate Finance</p><p>(FN)</p></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註Remarks</p></td><td colspan="16"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>各學程終端學習課程為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>The experiential learning course of each concentration is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>資訊軟體應用(CM115)、數位資料分析方法(CM263)、服務行銷與管理(CM304)、創業財務規劃(CM371)、數位創新與服務(CM245)、數位與行動商務(CM469)、人才培育與才能管理(CM384)、數位行銷傳播管理與應用(CM396)、數位與社群行銷(CM399)、數位經濟議題(CM477) 、數位轉型案例分析(CM249)、衍生性金融商品(CM327)、財務軟體應用(CM449)、財經數據分析方法(CM460)、網路爬蟲與人工智慧之投資應用(CM261)、Python程式設計(CM250)、資料採礦(CM252)、區塊鏈(CM253)、會計資訊系統(CM418)、電腦審計(CM488)、<strong>AI創新實踐與應用(CM271)</strong>為本院「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>    Introduction to Computer Software and Applications (CM115), Data Analysis Methods (CM263), Entrepreneurial Finance (CM371), Digital Innovation &amp; Service (CM245), Digital and Mobile Business (CM469), Talent Development and Competence Management (CM384), Digital Marketing Communication Management and application (CM396), Digital and Community Marketing (CM399), The Digital Economy (CM477), Case Study of Digital Transformation (CM249), Derivative Securities (CM327), Financial Packages and Applications (CM449), Financial Data Analysis (CM460), Web Crawler and Artificial Intelligence: The Application in Investment (CM261), Python Programming (CM250), Data Mining (CM252), Blockchain(CM253) , Accounting Information System (CM418), Computer Auditing (CM488) and <strong>AI Innovation Practice and Application (CM271)</strong>, are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本班同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院共同必修42學分、主修領域必修3-6學分、主修學程<strong>24-27</strong>學分（外系選修至多承認<strong>26-32</strong>學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。管院學士班之跨領域選修請參考第7條之規定。</li></ol><p>Student of BBA must take 128 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27), College Compulsory courses (42), Major Compulsory (3-6),and Concentration Subject(<strong>24-27</strong>). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (<strong>26-32</strong>) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit). If you choose elective credits of CM. Please refer to regulation 7 below for regulations regarding electives. </p><ol><li>學士班學生應選擇「企業管理」、「財務金融」、「國際企業」或「會計」為主修領域(Major Area)：</li><li>主修領域必修科目3或6學分：</li></ol><p>a.企業管理：學生應必修「作業管理」、「策略管理」</p><p>b.財務金融：學生應必修「投資學」、「公司理財」</p><p>c.國際企業：學生應必修「國際企業管理」</p><p>d.會計：學生應必修「中級會計學（一）」 </p><ol><li>管院主修學程科目<strong>24-27</strong>學分：</li></ol><p>a.企業管理：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>b.財務金融：學生應自「投資與企業金融學程」、「投資與風險管理學程」及「金融科技學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>c.國際企業：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>d.會計：學生應修習「會計專業學程」做為主修學程。</p><p>Students must choose one of the Major Areas and fulfill requirements of each major listed below:</p><ol><li>Major Areas and corresponding compulsory courses(3or6)</li><li>Business Administration：「Operations Management」、「Strategic Management」</li><li>Finance：「Investments」、「Corporate Finance」</li><li>International Business：「International Business Management」</li><li>Accounting：「Intermediate Accounting(I)」</li><li>Concentration courses (<strong>24-27</strong>)：</li><li>Students who major in Business Administration, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management” , “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing” and “International Business”.Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.</li><li>Students who major in Finance, 3 concentrations available: “Investment and Corporate Finance”, “Investment and Risk Management”and “FinTech”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in International Business, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management”, “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing”and “International Business”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Accounting can choose “Accounting Professional”as the major concentration.</li><li>管院學士班學生之跨領域選修規定：</li><li>學生除主修學程外，應符合下列任一輔修規定：</li></ol><p>a.輔修學程科目：修習另一學程三門課做為輔修學程(9學分)。</p><p>b.輔修產業學程科目：修習本院或跨院產業學程12學分做為輔修學程（12學分不得含管院共同必修）。</p><p>c.輔修跨院學程科目：修習他院12學分做為輔修學程(12學分須為同院課程)。</p><ol><li>完成主修學程修課規定之學生，符合前項a(輔修學程科目)及b(輔修產業學程科目)規定者，將於畢業證書上加註證明；符合前項c(輔修跨院學程科目)者，不另提供證明或證書。</li></ol><p>Regulations regarding electives: </p><ol><li>In addition to fulfilling the requirements of selected major and concentration, students also must satisfy one of the following requirements: </li><li>Concentration minor in CM: students should take 9 credits within each of their selected minor(s).</li><li>Industrial Program minor: students should take 12 credits within each of their selected industrial program(s) (excluding 12 credits of College Compulsory courses).</li><li>Minor outside CM: students should take 12 credits within a college.</li><li>Concentration minor in CM and Industrial Program minor will be certified on the diploma. Minor outside CM will not be certified. </li><li>學士班學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Students also need to complete Career Literacy credits in order to graduate. Please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport] for detailed information.</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必俢規定)</li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor ), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

Service”, “Digital and Mobile Business “ and “Business Management Practice and Seminar”.</p><p>Required courses for Minor:</p><ol><li>“Digital Innovation &amp; Service” or “Digital and Mobile Business” (1 out of 2).</li><li>“Innovation Management and Practice” or “Business Management Practice and Seminar” (1 out of 2).</li></ol><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 1 course out of remaining 12courses.</p></td></tr></table>

(3)</strong></p><p><strong>Cross-border Innovation and Growth</strong></p></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td><p>國貿實務</p><p>CM242(3)</p><p>Practice of International colspan="8"><p>說明：課程十四選<strong>八</strong> </p><p>主修必選－全球產業與分析、國際金融、國際企業經營決策、策略布局與商業模式新創實作（終端學習課程），以上<strong>四</strong>門均為國際企業學程必選。下述為建議選課模組，但不強制。</p><ol><li>全球化管理模式模組：全球電商與物流、國際人力資源管理、跨國界創新實務議題、市場競爭分析。</li><li>當代議題模組：新興市場議題、數位轉型案例分析、前瞻產業實務研究。</li><li>證照與技能模組：國貿實務、國際企業談判、管理決策模型。</li></ol><p>輔修必選－國際企業管理(主修領域為國際企業之學生，應另選一門學程選修課替代)、策略布局與商業模式新創實作</p><p>Note: </p><p>Course selection: choose <strong>eight</strong> out of fourteen.</p><p>Required courses for Concentration: “Global Industrial Analysis”，“International Finance”，“Strategic Management of Multinational Corporations”，“Practice in Strategic Formulation and Business Model Innovation” , the above <strong>four</strong> courses are required for the core module. The modules below are the suggestion of the courses selection. Just for reference and not mandatory.</p><ol><li>Management strategies for global businesses module :“Global E-Commerce and Logistics”、“International Human Resource Management”、“Cross-border Innovation and Growth”、<strong>“Market Competition Analysis”</strong></li><li>Contemporary issues module :“ Emerging Market Issues”、“ Case Study of Digital Transformation”、“Foresight Industries and Practices”</li><li>Certificate and skill module :“Practice of International Trade”、“International Business Negotiations”、“Decision Models for Management”</li></ol><p>Required courses for Minor: “International Business Management” and “Practice in Strategic Formulation and Business Model”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 1 course out of remaining 1<strong>3</strong> courses. If you are already a major in international business, you must choose an elective course instead of 'International Business Management'.</p></td></tr></table>

colspan="8"><p>說明：課程十四選<strong>八</strong></p><p>       主修必選－企業財務分析、金融倫理與法規、財務金融個案研討（終端學習課程）<strong>;若為雙主修本學程與「投資與風險管理」學程者，"金融倫理與法規"須以此二學程之其他選修課替代。</strong></p><p>　輔修－必選投資學，其餘任選兩門。若為財金主修<strong>或已輔修「投資與風險管理」學程者</strong>，則須任選三門。</p><p>Note: </p><p>Course selection: choose <strong>eight</strong> out of fourteen.</p><p>Required courses for Concentration: “Business Analysis Using Financial Statements”, “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”, and “Case Studies in Finance”. </p><p>Elective courses for Concentration: in addition to above required courses, choose a minimum of <strong>5</strong> courses out of remaining <strong>11</strong> courses.</p><p><strong>Students who double major in this Concentration and "Investment and Risk Management" Concentration are required to take one elective course in these two Concentrations to replace “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining 14 courses. Students who major in Finance <strong>or minor in "Investment and Risk Management"</strong>, choose a minimum of 3 courses out of remaining 14 courses.</p></td></tr></table>

colspan="8"><p>說明：課程十四選<strong>八</strong></p><p>      主修必選－衍生性金融商品、計量經濟學、風險管理、金融倫理與法規、投資組合與證券分析（終端學習課程）<strong>;若為雙主修本學程與「投資與企業金融」學程者，"金融倫理與法規"須以此二學程之其他選修課替代。</strong></p><p>輔修－必選投資學，其餘任選兩門。若為財金主修<strong>或已輔修「投資與企業金融」學程者</strong>，則須任選三門。</p><p>Note: </p><p>Course selection: choose <strong>eight</strong> out of fourteen.</p><p>Required courses for Concentration: “Derivative Securities”, “Econometrics”, “Risk Management”, “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”, and “Portfolio and Security Analysis”. </p><p>Elective courses for Concentration: in addition to above required courses, choose a minimum of<strong> 3</strong> courses out of remaining 9 courses.</p><p><strong>Students who double major in this Concentration and "Investment and Corporate Finance" Concentration are required to take one elective course in these two Concentrations to replace “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining 14 courses. Students who major in Finance <strong>or minor in "Investment and Corporate Finance"</strong>, choose a minimum of 3 courses out of remaining <strong>14</strong> courses.</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="12"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="12"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="12"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

colspan="2"></td><td><p>作業管理*</p><p>CM206( 3)</p><p>(國企管)</p><p>Operations Management</p><p>(BA&amp;IB)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="9"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>各學程終端學習課程為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>The experiential learning course of each concentration is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>資訊軟體應用(CM115)、數位資料分析方法(CM263)、服務行銷與管理(CM304)、創業財務規劃(CM371)、數位創新與服務(CM245)、數位與行動商務(CM469)、人才培育與才能管理(CM384)、數位行銷傳播管理與應用(CM396)、數位與社群行銷(CM399)、數位經濟議題(CM477) 、數位轉型案例分析(CM249)、衍生性金融商品(CM327)、財務軟體應用(CM449)、財經數據分析方法(CM460)、網路爬蟲與人工智慧之投資應用(CM261)、Python程式設計(CM250)、資料採礦(CM252)、區塊鏈(CM253)、會計資訊系統(CM418) 、電腦審計(CM488)、<strong>AI創新實踐與應用(CM271)</strong>為本院「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>    Introduction to Computer Software and Applications (CM115), Data Analysis Methods (CM263), Entrepreneurial Finance (CM371), Digital Innovation &amp; Service (CM245), Digital and Mobile Business (CM469), Talent Development and Competence Management (CM384), Digital Marketing Communication Management and application (CM396), Digital and Community Marketing (CM399), The Digital Economy (CM477), Case Study of Digital Transformation (CM249), Derivative Securities (CM327), Financial Packages and Applications (CM449), Financial Data Analysis (CM460), Web Crawler and Artificial Intelligence: The Application in Investment (CM261), Python Programming (CM250), Data Mining (CM252), Blockchain (CM253), Accounting Information System (CM418), <strong>Computer Auditing (CM488)</strong> and <strong>AI Innovation Practice and Application (CM271), </strong>are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本班同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院共同必修<strong>44</strong>學分、主修領域必修0-6學分、主修學程<strong>24-27</strong>學分（外系選修至多承認<strong>24-33</strong>學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。管院學士班之跨領域選修請參考第7條之規定。</li></ol><p>Student of BBA must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27), College Compulsory courses (42), Major Compulsory (0-6), and Concentration Subject (<strong>24-27</strong>). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (<strong>24-33</strong>) credits and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit). If you choose elective credits of CM. Please refer to regulation 7 below for regulations regarding electives. </p><ol><li>學士班學生應選擇「數位行銷與人力資源」、「財務金融」、「國際企業管理」或「會計」為主修領域(Major Area)：</li><li>主修領域必修科目0~6學分：</li><li>數位行銷與人力資源：無</li><li>財務金融：學生應必修「投資學」、「公司理財」</li><li>國際企業管理：學生應必修「作業管理」</li><li>會計：學生應必修「中級會計學（一）」 </li><li>管院主修學程科目<strong>24-27</strong>學分：</li></ol><p>a.數位行銷與人力資源：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>b.財務金融：學生應自「投資與企業金融學程」、「投資與風險管理學程」及「金融科技學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>c.國際企業管理：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>d.會計：學生應修習「會計專業學程」做為主修學程。</p><p>Students must choose one of the Major Areas and fulfill requirements of each major listed below:</p><ol><li>Major Areas and corresponding compulsory courses(0~6)</li><li>Digital Marketing and Human Resources：N/A</li><li>Finance：「Investments」、「Corporate Finance」</li><li>Business Administration &amp; International Business：「Operations Management」</li><li>Accounting：「Intermediate Accounting(I)」</li><li>Concentration courses (<strong>24-27</strong>)：</li><li>Students who major in Digital Marketing and Human Resources, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management” , “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing” and “International Business”.Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.</li><li>Students who major in Finance, 3 concentrations available: “Investment and Corporate Finance”, “Investment and Risk Management”and “FinTech”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Business Administration &amp; International Business, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management”, “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing”and “International Business”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Accounting can choose “Accounting Professional”as the major concentration. </li><li>管院學士班學生之跨領域選修規定：</li><li>學生除主修學程外，應符合下列任一輔修規定：</li></ol><p>a.輔修學程科目：修習另一學程三門課做為輔修學程(9學分)。</p><p>b.輔修產業學程科目：修習本院或跨院產業學程12學分做為輔修學程（12學分不得含管院共同必修）。</p><p>c.輔修跨院學程科目：修習他院12學分做為輔修學程(12學分須為同院課程)。</p><ol><li>完成主修學程修課規定之學生，符合前項a(輔修學程科目)及b(輔修產業學程科目)規定者，將於畢業證書上加註證明；符合前項c(輔修跨院學程科目)者，不另提供證明或證書。</li></ol><p>Regulations regarding electives: </p><ol><li>In addition to fulfilling the requirements of selected major and concentration, students also must satisfy one of the following requirements: </li><li>Concentration minor in CM: students should take 9 credits within each of their selected minor(s).</li><li>Industrial Program minor: students should take 12 credits within each of their selected industrial program(s) (excluding 12 credits of College Compulsory courses).</li><li>Minor outside CM: students should take 12 credits within a college.</li><li>Concentration minor in CM and Industrial Program minor will be certified on the diploma. Minor outside CM will not be certified. </li><li>學士班學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Students also need to complete Career Literacy credits in order to graduate. Please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport] for detailed information.</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必俢規定)</li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor ), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p></td></tr></table>

colspan="8"><p>說明：課程十<strong>七</strong>選<strong>八</strong></p><p>主修必選－國際企業管理、全球產業與分析、國際金融、國際企業經營決策、策略布局與商業模式新創實作（終端學習課程），以上<strong>五</strong>門均為國際企業學程必選。下述為建議選課模組，但不強制。</p><ol><li>全球化管理模式模組：全球電商與物流、國際人力資源管理、跨國界創新實務議題<strong>、服務行銷與管理、市場競爭分析</strong>。</li><li>當代議題模組：新興市場議題、數位轉型案例分析、前瞻產業實務研究<strong>、創新管理與實務</strong>。</li><li>證照與技能模組：國貿實務、國際企業談判、管理決策模型。</li></ol><p>輔修必選－國際企業管理、策略布局與商業模式新創實作</p><p>Note: </p><p>Course selection: choose <strong>eight</strong> out of seventeen.</p><p>Required courses for Concentration: “International Business Management”，“Global Industrial Analysis”，“International Finance”，“Strategic Management of Multinational Corporations”，“Practice in Strategic Formulation and Business Model Innovation” , the above <strong>five</strong> courses are required for the core module. The modules below are the suggestion of the courses selection. Just for reference and not mandatory.</p><ol><li>Management strategies for global businesses module :“Global E-Commerce and Logistics”、“International Human Resource Management”、“Cross-border Innovation and Growth”<strong> 、“Service Marketing and Management”、<s> </s>“Market Competition Analysis”</strong></li><li>Contemporary issues module :“ Emerging Market Issues”、“ Case Study of Digital Transformation”、“Foresight Industries and Practices”<strong> 、“Innovation Management and Practice”</strong></li><li>Certificate and skill module :“Practice of International Trade”、“International Business Negotiations”、“Decision Models for Management”</li></ol><p>Required courses for Minor: “International Business Management” and “Practice in Strategic Formulation and Business Model”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 1 course out of remaining 1<strong>5</strong> courses. </p></td></tr></table>

主修必選－企業財務分析、金融倫理與法規、財務金融個案研討（終端學習課程）<strong>;若為雙主修本學程與「投資與風險管理」學程者，"金融倫理與法規"須以此二學程之其他選修課替代。</strong></p><p>　輔修－必選投資學，其餘任選兩門。若為財金主修<strong>或已輔修「投資與風險管理」學程者</strong>，則須任選三門。</p><p>Note: </p><p>Course selection: choose <strong>eight</strong> out of thirteen.</p><p>Required courses for Concentration: “Business Analysis Using Financial Statements”, “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”, and “Case Studies in Finance”. </p><p>Elective courses for Concentration: in addition to above required courses, choose a minimum of <strong>5</strong> courses out of remaining <strong>10</strong> courses.</p><p><strong>Students who double major in this Concentration and "Investment and Risk Management" Concentration are required to take one elective course in these two Concentrations to replace “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining <strong>13</strong> courses. Students who major in Finance <strong>or minor in "Investment and Risk Management"</strong>, choose a minimum of 3 courses out of remaining <strong>13</strong> courses.</p></td></tr></table>

Securities Law”, and “Portfolio and Security Analysis”. </p><p>Elective courses for Concentration: in addition to above required courses, choose a minimum of <strong>3</strong> courses out of remaining 9 courses.</p><p><strong>Students who double major in this Concentration and "Investment and Corporate Finance" Concentration are required to take one elective course in these two Concentrations to replace “Financial Ethics and the Securities Law”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining 14 courses. 115.04.29一一四學年度第七次教務修訂通過

Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on April 29, 2026

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（一） Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression （I）（2）</p></td><td><p>中文閱讀、思辨與表達（二）Chinese Reading, Critical Thinking, and Expression （II）（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English （I）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>英語（二）</p><p>English （II）</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><ol><li>外語課程應修習 10 學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li><li>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程 10 學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li><li>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</li><li>English （I） &amp; （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> <strong>英語檢定English Testing （2）</strong>、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>備註Remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>各學程終端學習課程為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>The experiential learning course of each concentration is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>資訊軟體應用(CM115)、數位資料分析方法(CM263)、服務行銷與管理(CM304)、創業財務規劃(CM371)、數位創新與服務(CM245)、數位與行動商務(CM469)、人才培育與才能管理(CM384)、數位行銷傳播管理與應用(CM396)、數位與社群行銷(CM399)、數位經濟議題(CM477) 、數位轉型案例分析(CM249)、衍生性金融商品(CM327)、財務軟體應用(CM449)、財經數據分析方法(CM460)、網路爬蟲與人工智慧之投資應用(CM261)、Python程式設計(CM250)、資料採礦(CM252)、區塊鏈(CM253)、會計資訊系統(CM418) 、電腦審計(CM488) 、<strong>AI創新實踐與應用(CM271)</strong>為本院「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Introduction to Computer Software and Applications (CM115), Data Analysis Methods (CM263), Entrepreneurial Finance(CM371), Digital Innovation &amp; Service (CM245), Digital and Mobile Business (CM469), Talent Development and Competence Management (CM384), Digital Marketing Communication Management and application(CM396), Digital and Community Marketing (CM399), The Digital Economy (CM477), Case Study of Digital Transformation(CM249), Derivative Securities (CM327), Financial Packages and Applications (CM449), Financial Data Analysis (CM460), Web Crawler and Artificial Intelligence: The Application in Investment(CM261), Python Programming(CM250), Data Mining(CM252), Blockchain(CM253), Accounting Information System(CM418), Computer Auditing(CM488) and <strong>AI Innovation Practice and Application(CM271), </strong>are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本班同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院共同必修42學分、主修學程24-30學分、輔修學程9-12學分（外系選修至多承認<strong>17-26</strong>學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。管院學士班之跨領域選修請參考第7條之規定。</li></ol><p>Student of BBA must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27), College Compulsory courses (44), Concentration Subject (24-30) , and Concentration minor (9-12). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the <strong>(17-26) </strong>credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit). If you choose elective credits of BBA, Please refer to regulation 7 below for regulations regarding electives. </p><ol><li>學士班學生應選擇「數位行銷與人力資源」、「財務金融」、「國際企業管理」或「會計」為主修領域(Major Area)：</li></ol><p>管院主修學程科目24-30學分：</p><p>a.數位行銷與人力資源：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>b.財務金融：學生應自「投資與企業金融學程」、「投資與風險管理學程」及「金融科技學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>c.國際企業管理：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>d.會計：學生應修習「會計專業學程」做為主修學程。</p><p>Students must choose one of the Major Areas and fulfill requirements of each major listed below:</p><p>Concentration courses (24-30)：</p><ol><li>Students who major in Digital Marketing and Human Resources, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management”, “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing” and “International Business”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.</li><li>Students who major in Finance, 3 concentrations available: “Investment and Corporate Finance”, “Investment and Risk Management” and “FinTech”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Business Administration &amp; International Business, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management”, “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing” and “International Business”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Accounting can choose “Accounting Professional” as the major concentration. </li><li>管院學士班學生之跨領域選修規定：</li><li>學生除主修學程外，應符合下列任一輔修規定：</li></ol><p>a.輔修學程科目：修習另一學程三門課做為輔修學程(9學分)。</p><p>b.輔修產業學程科目：修習本院或跨院產業學程12學分做為輔修學程（12學分不得含管院共同必修）。</p><p>c.輔修跨院學程科目：修習他院12學分做為輔修學程(12學分須為同院課程)。</p><ol><li>完成主修學程修課規定之學生，符合前項a(輔修學程科目)及b(輔修產業學程科目)規定者，將於畢業證書上加註證明；符合前項c(輔修跨院學程科目)者，不另提供證明或證書。</li></ol><p>Regulations regarding electives: </p><ol><li>In addition to fulfilling the requirements of selected major and concentration, students also must satisfy one of the following requirements: </li><li>Concentration minor in CM: students should take 9 credits within each of their selected minor(s).</li><li>Industrial Program minor: students should take 12 credits within each of their selected industrial program(s) (excluding 12 credits of College Compulsory courses).</li><li>Minor outside CM: students should take 12 credits within a college.</li><li>Concentration minor in CM and Industrial Program minor will be certified on the diploma. Minor outside CM will not be certified. </li><li>學士班學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Students also need to complete Career Literacy credits in order to graduate. Please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport] for detailed information.</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必修規定)</li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學士班規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor ), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by BBA program.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4 版)／113.12.16 修訂

Concentration and "Investment and Risk Management" Concentration or "FinTech" Concentration are required to take another elective course in these three Concentrations to replace “Investments”,“Corporate Finance”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: in addition to one required course, choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining <strong>14 </strong>courses. Students who major in Finance <strong>or minor in "Investment and Risk Management" Concentration or"FinTech" Concentration</strong>, choose a minimum of 3 courses out of remaining 1<strong>5</strong> courses.</p></td></tr></table>

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> <strong>英語檢定English Testing （2）</strong>、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr></table>

<table><tr><td><p>備註Remarks</p></td><td><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>各學程終端學習課程為必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>The experiential learning course of each concentration is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>資訊軟體應用(CM115)、數位資料分析方法(CM263)、服務行銷與管理(CM304)、創業財務規劃(CM371)、數位創新與服務(CM245)、數位與行動商務(CM469)、人才培育與才能管理(CM384)、數位行銷傳播管理與應用(CM396)、數位與社群行銷(CM399)、數位經濟議題(CM477) 、數位轉型案例分析(CM249)、衍生性金融商品(CM327)、財務軟體應用(CM449)、財經數據分析方法(CM460)、網路爬蟲與人工智慧之投資應用(CM261)、Python程式設計(CM250)、資料採礦(CM252)、區塊鏈(CM253)、會計資訊系統(CM418) 、電腦審計(CM488) 、<strong>AI創新實踐與應用(CM271)</strong>為本院「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Introduction to Computer Software and Applications (CM115), Data Analysis Methods (CM263), Entrepreneurial Finance(CM371), Digital Innovation &amp; Service (CM245), Digital and Mobile Business (CM469), Talent Development and Competence Management (CM384), Digital Marketing Communication Management and application(CM396), Digital and Community Marketing (CM399), The Digital Economy (CM477), Case Study of Digital Transformation(CM249), Derivative Securities (CM327), Financial Packages and Applications (CM449), Financial Data Analysis (CM460), Web Crawler and Artificial Intelligence: The Application in Investment(CM261), Python Programming(CM250), Data Mining(CM252), Blockchain(CM253), Accounting Information System(CM418), Computer Auditing(CM488) and <strong>AI Innovation Practice and Application(CM271), </strong>are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本班同學總共必須修滿128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院共同必修42學分、主修學程24-30學分、輔修學程9-12學分（外系選修至多承認<strong>17-26</strong>學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。管院學士班之跨領域選修請參考第7條之規定。</li></ol><p>Student of BBA must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27), College Compulsory courses (44), Concentration Subject (24-30) , and Concentration minor (9-12). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the <strong>(17-26) </strong>credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit). If you choose elective credits of BBA, Please refer to regulation 7 below for regulations regarding electives. </p><ol><li>學士班學生應選擇「數位行銷與人力資源」、「財務金融」、「國際企業管理」或「會計」為主修領域(Major Area)：</li></ol><p>管院主修學程科目24-30學分：</p><p>a.數位行銷與人力資源：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>b.財務金融：學生應自「投資與企業金融學程」、「投資與風險管理學程」及「金融科技學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>c.國際企業管理：學生應自「企業管理學程」、「領導暨人力資源學程」、「行銷學程」及「國際企業學程」中擇一做為主修學程。</p><p>d.會計：學生應修習「會計專業學程」做為主修學程。</p><p>Students must choose one of the Major Areas and fulfill requirements of each major listed below:</p><p>Concentration courses (24-30)：</p><ol><li>Students who major in Digital Marketing and Human Resources, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management”, “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing” and “International Business”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.</li><li>Students who major in Finance, 3 concentrations available: “Investment and Corporate Finance”, “Investment and Risk Management” and “FinTech”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Business Administration &amp; International Business, 4 concentrations available: “Business Management”, “Leadership &amp; Human Resources”, “Marketing” and “International Business”. Students should choose a minimum of one as the major concentration.  </li><li>Students who major in Accounting can choose “Accounting Professional” as the major concentration. </li><li>管院學士班學生之跨領域選修規定：</li><li>學生除主修學程外，應符合下列任一輔修規定：</li></ol><p>a.輔修學程科目：修習另一學程三門課做為輔修學程(9學分)。</p><p>b.輔修產業學程科目：修習本院或跨院產業學程12學分做為輔修學程（12學分不得含管院共同必修）。</p><p>c.輔修跨院學程科目：修習他院12學分做為輔修學程(12學分須為同院課程)。</p><ol><li>完成主修學程修課規定之學生，符合前項a(輔修學程科目)及b(輔修產業學程科目)規定者，將於畢業證書上加註證明；符合前項c(輔修跨院學程科目)者，不另提供證明或證書。</li></ol><p>Regulations regarding electives: </p><ol><li>In addition to fulfilling the requirements of selected major and concentration, students also must satisfy one of the following requirements: </li><li>Concentration minor in CM: students should take 9 credits within each of their selected minor(s).</li><li>Industrial Program minor: students should take 12 credits within each of their selected industrial program(s) (excluding 12 credits of College Compulsory courses).</li><li>Minor outside CM: students should take 12 credits within a college.</li><li>Concentration minor in CM and Industrial Program minor will be certified on the diploma. Minor outside CM will not be certified. </li><li>學士班學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Students also need to complete Career Literacy credits in order to graduate. Please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport] for detailed information.</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必修規定)</li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學士班規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor ), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by BBA program.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

Concentration and "Investment and Risk Management" Concentration or "FinTech" Concentration are required to take another elective course in these three Concentrations to replace “Investments”,“Corporate Finance”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: in addition to one required course, choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining <strong>14 </strong>courses. Students who major in Finance <strong>or minor in "Investment and Risk Management" Concentration or"FinTech" Concentration</strong>, choose a minimum of 3 courses out of remaining 1<strong>5</strong> courses.</p></td></tr></table>

Management</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>說明：課程十<strong>五</strong>選十</p><p>      主修必選－投資學、公司理財、計量經濟學、衍生性金融商品、投資組合與證券分析（終端學習課程）<strong>; 若為雙主修本學程與「投資與企業金融」學程或「金融科技」學程者， "投資學"、"公司理財"須以此三學程之其他選修課替代。</strong></p><p>　輔修－必選投資學，其餘任選兩門。若為財金主修<strong>或已輔修「投資與企業金融」學程或已輔修「金融科技」學程者</strong>，則須任選三門。</p><p>Note: </p><p>Course selection: choose ten out of fifteen.</p><p>Required courses for Concentration: “Investments”,“Corporate Finance”, “Econometrics”, “Derivative Securities”,and “Portfolio and Security Analysis”. </p><p>Elective courses for Concentration: in addition to five required courses, choose a minimum of <strong>5</strong> courses out of remaining 10 courses.</p><p><strong>Students who double major in this Concentration and "</strong> <strong>Investment and Corporate Finance " Concentration or "FinTech" Concentration are required to take another elective course in these three Concentrations to replace “Investments”,“Corporate Finance”.</strong></p><p>Required courses for Minor: “Investments”</p><p>Elective courses for Minor: in addition to one required course, choose a minimum of 2 courses out of remaining 1<strong>4</strong> courses. Students who major in Finance <strong>or minor in "</strong> <strong>Investment and Corporate Finance " Concentration or"FinTech" Concentration</strong>, choose a minimum of 3 courses out of remaining 1<strong>5</strong> courses.</p></td></tr></table>

**Yuan Ze University, College of Management EBBA Program**

**List of Required Courses**

**（110學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2021)**

112.11.22 一一二學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on November 22, 2023

students are required to obtain.</p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>英語檢定 English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p><a></a>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses, students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>（10）</p><p>General Education</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>其餘2學分學生修習通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic CM449), course “Derivative Securities” (Course code CM327), course” Service Marketing and Management” (course code CM304), course” Global Industrial Analysis” (course code CM219) ,Entrepreneurial Finance (course code CM371)  are courses of digital application courses'. Students require taking at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>校共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修科目42學分、主修領域必修科目6學分、語言素養科目8學分、及主修學程科目27學分(國際財務金融學程或全球經營管理學程二選一)。</li></ol><p>University compulsory courses (17), General Education courses (10), College compulsory courses (42), concentration compulsory courses (6), language width (8), Program Subject (27) (either Global Business Management or International Finance)</p><ol><li>學生得輔修學程科目9學分或產業學程科目12學分，課程內容請參考學士班選修科目表</li><li>凡學生修習主修學程、輔修學程及產業學程內之任一課程科目相同者皆不可重複採計認列學分數。</li><li>學生依學程規定取得主輔修學程將於畢業證書上加註證明；產業學程則另授予證書。</li></ol><p>Students could take other Program subject (9) or industrial program subject (12) as their minor should refer to the College of Management’s BBA regulations for the list of selective courses.</p><p>(1) Student’s score of any course taking from either major Program subject, minor Program subject, or industrial program subject could not be double-counted.</p><p>(2) Students taking courses from either major Program subject or minor Program subject will be noted in diploma; Credits earned by taking the courses from industrial program subject will be awarded the certificate.</p><ol><li>學士班之擋修規定，另依據管理學院學士班擋修科目表之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to College of Management’s BBA regulations for the list of course prerequisites.</p><ol><li>外籍生通識科目(31)依照校內外籍學生之校必修通識規定辦理。</li></ol><p>For foreign students, please refer to General Education Courses Information and Regulations.</p><ol><li>學生需於畢業前有國際研習的經驗，始滿足畢業的要求，有關國際研習的規定，請參考『元智大學管理學院學士英語專班「國際研習」辦法』。</li></ol><p>Local Students should participate in international integrated learning activities and meet the requirements for graduation. Please refer to College of Management’s EBBA Essentials for the International Integrated Learning.</p><ol><li>總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</li></ol><p>128 total credits for graduation.</p><ol><li>學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Local Students need to complete Career Literacy, for details regarding this course, please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport]。</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必俢規定) </li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>「為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor’s students), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.」</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學　管理學院學士英語專班 必修科目表**

**Yuan Ze University, College of Management EBBA Program**

**List of Required Courses**

**（111學年度入學新生適用）**

112.11.22 一一二學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on November 22, 2023

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p><p>First Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p><p>Second Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年</p><p>Third Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年</p><p>Fourth Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="6"><p>共同必修</p><p>科目</p><p>Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>英語檢定 English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p><a></a>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>（10）</p><p>General Education</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>其餘2學分學生修習通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic 112.11.22 一一二學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on November 22, 2023

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p><p>First Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p><p>Second Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年</p><p>Third Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年</p><p>Fourth Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td><td><p>下2<sup>nd</sup></p></td><td><p>上1<sup>st</sup></p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="6"><p>共同必修</p><p>科目</p><p>Common Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>英語檢定 English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p><a></a>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>（10）</p><p>General Education</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>其餘2學分學生修習通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic colspan="6"><p>第二外語課程(8)，共計四學期8學分，畢業前需修畢一第二外語，始取得畢業資格。</p><p>Second foreign language curriculum (8), 8 credits for four semesters, one second foreign language for graduation.</p><p>已取得第二外語(限日、韓、德、法、西文)檢定考試通過者，得依照【元智大學管理學院學士英語專班『第二外語』抵免辦法】提出抵換修申請，抵免之後的學分，可自由選修其他課程(通識除外)。Those who have passed the second foreign language test (Japanese, Korean, German, French, and Spanish only) can apply for a replacement program in accordance with the "Course Substitution of Second Foreign Language Method “ for EBBA Program of Yuan Ze University, and can be replaced by other elective courses (except G.E. course).</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remark</p><p>全文完</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>衍生性金融商品(課號CM327)、國際企業策略個案(課號CM445)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分。</li></ol><p>Derivative Securities (Course code CM327) or Case Studies of Strategic Decision-Making in International Business (Course code CM445)is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>資訊軟體應用(課號CM115)、財務軟體應用(課號CM449)、衍生性金融商品(CM327)、服務行銷與管理(課號CM304)、全球產業分析(課號CM219) 、創業財務規劃(課號CM371) 、Python 程式設計(課號CM250)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須修習至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本院或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Course “Computer Software and Applications” (course code CM115), course “Financial Packages and Applications” (course code CM449), course “Derivative Securities” (Course code CM327), course” Service Marketing and Management” (course code CM304), course” Global Industrial Analysis” (course code CM219) ,Entrepreneurial Finance (course code CM371) , Python Programming (course code CM250) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require taking at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>校共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修科目44學分、主修領域必修科目6學分、語言素養科目8學分、及主修學程科目27學分(國際財務金融學程或全球經營管理學程二選一)。</li></ol><p>University compulsory courses (17), General Education courses (10), College compulsory courses (44), concentration compulsory courses (6), language width (8), Program Subject (27) (either Global Business Management or International Finance)</p><ol><li>學生得輔修學程科目9學分或產業學程科目12學分，課程內容請參考學士班選修科目表</li><li>凡學生修習主修學程、輔修學程及產業學程內之任一課程科目相同者皆不可重複採計認列學分數。</li><li>學生依學程規定取得主輔修學程將於畢業證書上加註證明；產業學程則另授予證書。</li></ol><p>Students could take other Program subject (9) or industrial program subject (12) as their minor should refer to the College of Management’s BBA regulations for the list of selective courses.</p><p>(1) Student’s score of any course taking from either major Program subject, minor Program subject, or industrial program subject could not be double-counted.</p><p>(2) Students taking courses from either major Program subject or minor Program subject will be noted in diploma; Credits earned by taking the courses from industrial program subject will be awarded the certificate.</p><ol><li>學士班之擋修規定，另依據管理學院學士班擋修科目表之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to College of Management’s BBA regulations for the list of course prerequisites.</p><ol><li>外籍生通識科目(31)依照校內外籍學生之校必修通識規定辦理。</li></ol><p>For foreign students, please refer to General Education Courses Information and Regulations.</p><ol><li>學生需於畢業前有國際研習的經驗，始滿足畢業的要求，有關國際研習的規定，請參考『元智大學管理學院學士英語專班「國際研習」辦法』。</li></ol><p>Local Students should participate in international integrated learning activities and meet the requirements for graduation. Please refer to College of Management’s EBBA Essentials for the International Integrated Learning.</p><ol><li>總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</li></ol><p>128 total credits for graduation.</p><ol><li>學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Local Students need to complete Career Literacy, for details regarding this course, please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport]。</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必俢規定) </li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>「為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor’s students), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.」</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p></td></tr></table>

**Yuan Ze University, College of Management EBBA Program**

**List of Required Courses**

**（113學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2024)**

Amended by the 9th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on June 05, 2024

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>英語檢定 English Testing（2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）   </p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p><a></a>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>（10）</p><p>General Education</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>其餘2學分學生修習通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Spanish only) can apply for a replacement program in accordance with the "Course Substitution of Second Foreign Language <strong>Method</strong> “ for EBBA Program of Yuan Ze University, and can be replaced by other elective courses (except G.E. course).</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>remark</p><p>全文完</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>衍生性金融商品(課號CM327)、國際企業策略個案(課號CM445)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分。</li></ol><p>Derivative Securities (Course code CM327) or Case Studies of Strategic Decision-Making in International Business (Course code CM445)is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>資訊軟體應用(課號CM115)、財務軟體應用(課號CM449)、衍生性金融商品(CM327)、服務行銷與管理(課號CM304)、全球產業分析(課號CM219) 、創業財務規劃(課號CM371) 、Python 程式設計(課號CM250)為本班「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須修習至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本院或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Course “Computer Software and Applications” (course code CM115), course “Financial Packages and Applications” (course code CM449), course “Derivative Securities” (Course code CM327), course” Service Marketing and Management” (course code CM304), course” Global Industrial Analysis” (course code CM219) ,Entrepreneurial Finance (course code CM371) , Python Programming (course code CM250) are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require taking at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>校共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修科目42學分、語言素養科目8學分、及主修學程科目33學分(國際財務金融學程或全球經營管理學程二選一)。</li></ol><p>University compulsory courses (17), General Education courses (10), College compulsory courses (42), language width (8), Program Subject (33) (either Global Business Management or International Finance)</p><ol><li>學生得輔修學程科目9學分或產業學程科目12學分，課程內容請參考學士班選修科目表</li><li>凡學生修習主修學程、輔修學程及產業學程內之任一課程科目相同者皆不可重複採計認列學分數。</li><li>學生依學程規定取得主輔修學程將於畢業證書上加註證明；產業學程則另授予證書。</li></ol><p>Students could take other Program subject (9) or industrial program subject (12) as their minor should refer to the College of Management’s BBA regulations for the list of selective courses.</p><p>(1) Student’s score of any course taking from either major Program subject, minor Program subject, or industrial program subject could not be double-counted.</p><p>(2) Students taking courses from either major Program subject or minor Program subject will be noted in diploma; Credits earned by taking the courses from industrial program subject will be awarded the certificate.</p><ol><li>學士班之擋修規定，另依據管理學院學士班擋修科目表之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to College of Management’s BBA regulations for the list of course prerequisites.</p><ol><li>外籍生通識科目依照校內外籍學生之校必修通識規定辦理。</li></ol><p>For foreign students, please refer to General Education Courses Information and Regulations.</p><ol><li>學生需於畢業前有國際研習的經驗，始滿足畢業的要求，有關國際研習的規定，請參考『元智大學管理學院學士英語專班「國際研習」辦法』。</li></ol><p>Local Students should participate in international integrated learning activities and meet the requirements for graduation. Please refer to College of Management’s EBBA Essentials for the International Integrated Learning.</p><ol><li>總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</li></ol><p>128 total credits for graduation.</p><ol><li>學生須於畢業前修畢職涯素養，詳細修課方式請參閱管院職涯辦公室「元智大學管理學院職涯護照實施辦法」。</li></ol><p>Local Students need to complete Career Literacy, for details regarding this course, please check the [Yuan Ze College of Management Career Path Planning Passport]。</p><ol><li>星號(*)課程為EMI (English as Medium of Instruction)英語授課專業課程(依各主修學程必俢規定) </li></ol><p>Courses with * are EMI courses ( required by each major area.)</p><ol><li>「為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor’s students), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.」</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>
